1112        <!-- Shortcuts Samples -->
1113
1114
1115        <!-- This section of sample code shows how your application can add shortcuts to -->
1116        <!-- the launcher (home screen).  Shortcuts have a three step life cycle. -->
1117
1118
1119        <!-- 1.  Your application offers to provide shortcuts to the launcher.  When -->
1120        <!-- the user installs a shortcut, an activity within your application -->
1121        <!-- generates the actual shortcut and returns it to the launcher, where it -->
1122        <!-- is shown to the user as an icon. -->
1123
1124
1125        <!-- 2.  Any time the user clicks on an installed shortcut, an intent is sent. -->
1126        <!-- Typically this would then be handled as necessary by an activity within -->
1127        <!-- your application. -->
1128
1129
1130        <!-- 3.  The shortcut is deleted.  There is no notification to your application. -->
1131
1132
1133        <!-- In order provide shortcuts from your application, you provide three things: -->
1134
1135
1136        <!-- 1.  An intent-filter declaring your ability to provide shortcuts -->
1137        <!-- 2.  Code within the activity to provide the shortcuts as requested -->
1138        <!-- 3.  Code elsewhere within your activity, if appropriate, to receive -->
1139        <!-- intents from the shortcut itself. -->
1140
1141        <activity
